An analysis of the top Bigs (4s & 5s) in the 2017 NBA Draft.

A cosine similarity is computed between each prospect and NBA player, using both their per 40 minutes and advanced statistics from their NCAA seasons (collected from sports-reference.com).

The NBA players collected are every top 5 pick since 1993 that played in the NCAA, every all-star or all-NBA drafted since 1993, as well as certain exceptions from recent drafts for proper 'modern NBA' comparisons of players who are currently contributing to an NBA team.
